## Evidence Report: `add /api/v1/status/label_cardinality`

### Task COV (from twin_context)
```
["ROUTE"]   — confidence 0.51, ambiguous
```

No confident twin candidates matched. The index has no file-level cluster data for `api.go` (cluster count = 0). All subsequent evidence is from direct source inspection.

---

### Current State (VERIFIED from source)

| Claim | Evidence | Status |
|---|---|---|
| Route registration lives in `api.go` at L430–L469 | `api.go:430-469` | **VERIFIED** |
| Label endpoints use `wrapAgent` and `Queryable.Querier()` | `api.go:441-443` (`wrapAgent(api.labelNames)`, `wrapAgent(api.labelValues)`) | **VERIFIED** |
| Existing status routes are at `/status/*` prefix, also using `wrapAgent` | `api.go:460-464` (`/status/tsdb`, `/status/tsdb/blocks`, etc.) | **VERIFIED** |
| `labelNames` handler pattern: parse time/limit/matchers → `api.Queryable.Querier(mint, maxt)` → `q.LabelNames()` | `api.go:759-834` | **VERIFIED** |
| `labelValues` handler pattern: same + `route.Param(ctx, "name")` → `q.LabelValues()` | `api.go:836-931` | **VERIFIED** |
| `Querier` interface only exposes `LabelNames`, `LabelValues`, `Select` — **no cardinality method** | `storage/interface.go:123-132` (Querier embeds LabelQuerier + Select) | **VERIFIED** |
| `LabelQuerier` has no cardinality method | `storage/interface.go:175-189` | **VERIFIED** |
| Cardinality data exists on `TSDBAdminStats.Stats()` → `index.PostingsStats` via `api.db` | `api.go:213` (TSDBAdminStats interface), `tsdb/head.go:1547-1554` (Stats()), `tsdb/index/postings.go:188-194` (PostingsStats struct) | **VERIFIED** |
| `/status/tsdb` already calls `api.db.Stats()` and renders CardinalityMetricsStats, CardinalityLabelStats, etc. | `api.go:1915-1958` (serveTSDBStatus) | **VERIFIED** |

### Historical Context

- **HYPOTHESIS**: The `/status/tsdb` endpoint was designed as a catch-all for TSDB statistics including cardinality, which is why no dedicated label_cardinality endpoint exists.
- **HYPOTHESIS**: Adding cardinality to `storage.Querier` would require extending `LabelQuerier` interface + updating every Querier implementation (mergeGenericQuerier, secondaryQuerier, noopQuerier, remote.querier, mockQuerier) — high cross-boundary impact.
- **UNKNOWN**: Whether the original design intentionally avoided exposing raw cardinality per label through the Querier path (performance concerns with O(n*m) label iteration).

---

### Seam Recommendation

There are no direct `api.go` cluster seams in the index data. From source analysis:

- **Lowest-risk seam**: Place the new route at `api.go:444-445` (between existing label/series routes and `/status/*` routes). The handler function should go next to `serveTSDBStatus` at `api.go:1915+`.
- **Cross-boundary warning**: Extending `storage.Querier` or `storage.LabelQuerier` is a high-seam operation touching 7+ files across 4 packages (`storage`, `tsdb`, `storage/remote`, etc.)

---

### 5-Step Actionability Checklist

**Step 1 — Add route registration** (`api.go:~443`)
```
r.Get("/status/label_cardinality", wrapAgent(api.labelCardinality))
```
Place immediately after `r.Get("/label/:name/values", ...)` at line 443 and before `/series` at line 445.

**Step 2 — Choose implementation path: two options**

| Path | Cross-boundary impact | Performance | Files touched |
|---|---|---|---|
| **A. `api.db.Stats()` (TSDBAdminStats)** | None — reuses existing `db` field | Fast (cached in Head) | `api.go` only |
| **B. New `Querier.LabelCardinality()` method** | High — extend `LabelQuerier` + 7+ implementations | Can be optimized per engine | 7+ files across `storage/`, `tsdb/`, `storage/remote/` |

**Recommendation: Path A** — the `api.db.Stats()` path has zero cross-boundary impact and is already established by the `/status/tsdb` precedent.

**Step 3 — Implement handler** (`api.go`, new function next to `serveTSDBStatus` at ~L1915)

Pattern: call `api.db.Stats(statsByLabelName, limit)`, return a `labelCardinalityResponse` struct with per-label stats. Use the same `apiFuncResult` return type.

**Step 4 — Define response types** (in `api.go` or a new types file)

Minimal struct:
```go
type labelCardinalityResponse struct {
    LabelValueCountByLabelName      []TSDBStat `json:"label_value_count_by_label_name"`
    SeriesCountByLabelValuePair    []TSDBStat `json:"series_count_by_label_value_pair"`
}
```

Reuse existing `TSDBStat` struct already defined in the same file.

**Step 5 — Add tests** (`api_test.go`)

Follow the pattern of `TestAPIEndpoints` / `TestServeTSDBStatus`. Test with a mock `TSDBAdminStats` returning known `PostingsStats`. Verify both happy path and `db.Stats()` error path.

---

### Summary

- The `storage.Querier` path has **no cardinality method** — using it would require extending `LabelQuerier` (high cross-boundary impact, 7+ files)
- The **safest path** is `api.db.Stats()` via the existing `TSDBAdminStats` field, following the exact pattern of `serveTSDBStatus` (0 new cross-boundary edges)
- Route goes at `api.go:L444`, handler at `api.go:~L1960`, response structs reuse existing `TSDBStat`
- This is a single-file change (`api.go`) with no interface/implementation spread
